RUMOUR, MICROSTORY #1:
         NARRATIVE OF #I:
         7.00pm, the corridor: #I is talking with #F.
         #I segues to fretting about the next round of 'Home Office Hearings'.
         The conversation takes place one-on-one. No one overhears.

         The conversation takes place one-on-one. No one overhears.

RUMOUR, MICROSTORY #3:
         NARRATIVE OF #I:

         #I has a longstanding vendetta against #F.
         The conversation takes place one-on-one. No one overhears.
         * SOVIET GRANDEE: #F.

         7.02pm, the corridor: #I is talking with #F.
         They are reflecting on recent rumours circulated in the printed press.
         #I, confronting #F directly, segues to insinuating {SOVIET GRANDEE} is a party higher-up with distinctly Soviet leanings.
         #I has a longstanding vendetta against #F.
         The conversation takes place one-on-one. No one overhears.
         * SOVIET GRANDEE: #F.
         Later, in 7.11pm, the corridor: #I is talking with #F, #R, #S.
         They are making small talk about The Ashes.
         #F segues to divulging that {MARXIST STUDENT} was in a Marxist reading group back at Balliol.
         #I can tell #F is lying about #H being the 'MARXIST STUDENT' in their midst (earlier, #I told #F this was actually #K).
         The conversation takes place openly. Still, no one overhears.
         * MARXIST STUDENT: #H.
         Later, in 7.15pm, the lounge: #H is talking with #E, #M.
         They are making small talk about The Ashes.
         #H segues to saying that {#K}'s got a 'star witness' ready to names names, by all accounts.
         The conversation takes place openly. #I overhears.
         * #K: #K.
         * STAR WITNESS: UNIDENTIFIED.
         Later, in 7.19pm, the dining room: #I is talking with #O.
         They are insinuating {SOVIET GRANDEE} is a party higher-up with distinctly Soviet leanings.
         #O segues to regretting how terribly this reflects on {#a}'s stewardship, and {#A} before him.
         The conversation takes place one-on-one. No one overhears.
         * #a: #a.
         * #A: #A.
         Later, in 7.27pm, the kitchens: #I is talking with #A, #B, #H.
         They are ruminating on {#K}'s very public allegations that Communists have penetrated the upper echelons of Her Majesty's government.
         #A segues to reflecting on recent rumours circulated in the printed press.
         The conversation takes place behind closed doors, with no one else around. No one overhears.

MEET THE CANDIDATES, MICROSTORY #8:
         NARRATIVE OF #I:
         7.02pm, the corridor: #I is talking with #F.

         #F segues to divulging that {MARXIST STUDENT} was in a Marxist reading group back at Balliol.
         #I can tell #F is lying about #H being the 'MARXIST STUDENT' in their midst (earlier, #I told #F this was actually #K).
         The conversation takes place openly. Still, no one overhears.

         Later, in 7.15pm, the lounge: #H is talking with #E, #M.
         They are making small talk about The Ashes.
         #H segues to saying that {#K}'s got a 'star witness' ready to names names, by all accounts.
         The conversation takes place openly. #I overhears.

         * STAR WITNESS: UNIDENTIFIED.
         Later, in 7.19pm, the dining room: #I is talking with #O.
         They are insinuating {SOVIET GRANDEE} is a party higher-up with distinctly Soviet leanings.
         #O segues to regretting how terribly this reflects on {#a}'s stewardship, and {#A} before him.
         The conversation takes place one-on-one. No one overhears.
         * #a: #a.
         * #A: #A.
         Later, in 7.40pm, the kitchens: #I is talking with #A, #B, #G, #H, #J.
         They are stating that these anti-communism hearings are all part of a conspiracy to undermine the party.
         #A segues to asserting that the only people testifying against the cabinet have their own eyes on the leadership.
         The conversation takes place behind closed doors, with no one else around. No one overhears.
         * STAR WITNESS: UNIDENTIFIED.

         They are making small talk about The Ashes.
         #F segues to divulging that {MARXIST STUDENT} was in a Marxist reading group back at Balliol.
         #I can tell #F is lying about #H being the 'MARXIST STUDENT' in their midst (earlier, #I told #F this was actually #K).
         The conversation takes place openly. Still, no one overhears.
         * MARXIST STUDENT: #H.
         Later, in 7.16pm, the downstairs: #I is talking with #J, #K.
         They are speculating that whomever is leaking against the government must be part of the fifth column, so vicious they are in their subversive activities.
         #K segues to regretting how terribly this reflects on {#a}'s stewardship, and {#A} before him.
         #I knows #K has longstanding vendettas against #a, #A.
         The conversation takes place openly. Still, no one overhears.
         * #a: #a.
         * #A: #A.
         Later, in 7.22pm, the downstairs: #H is talking with #J.
         They are asserting that the only people testifying against the cabinet have their own eyes on the leadership.
         #H segues to worrying about threats to the party, within and without.
         The conversation takes place one-on-one. Still, #I overhears.
         Later, in 7.40pm, the kitchens: #I is talking with #A, #B, #G, #H, #J.
         They are stating that these anti-communism hearings are all part of a conspiracy to undermine the party.
         #A segues to asserting that the only people testifying against the cabinet have their own eyes on the leadership.
         The conversation takes place behind closed doors, with no one else around. No one overhears.
         * STAR WITNESS: UNIDENTIFIED.

         #I, confronting #F directly, segues to insinuating {SOVIET GRANDEE} is a party higher-up with distinctly Soviet leanings.
         #I has a longstanding vendetta against #F.
         The conversation takes place one-on-one. No one overhears.
         * SOVIET GRANDEE: #F.
         Later, in 7.11pm, the corridor: #I is talking with #F, #R, #S.
         They are making small talk about The Ashes.
         #F segues to divulging that {MARXIST STUDENT} was in a Marxist reading group back at Balliol.
         #I can tell #F is lying about #H being the 'MARXIST STUDENT' in their midst (earlier, #I told #F this was actually #K).
         The conversation takes place openly. Still, no one overhears.
         * MARXIST STUDENT: #H.
         Later, in 7.22pm, the downstairs: #H is talking with #J.
         They are asserting that the only people testifying against the cabinet have their own eyes on the leadership.
         #H segues to worrying about threats to the party, within and without.
         The conversation takes place one-on-one. Still, #I overhears.
         Later, in 7.25pm, the dining room: #I is talking with #O.
         They are spreading that several party grandees - {GRANDEE #1} and {GRANDEE #2} amongst them - are losing confidence in {#a}.
         #O segues to suggesting {#A} organised this evening as his grand return to politics (a rumour hitherto unheard by #I).
         The conversation takes place one-on-one. No one overhears.
         * #A: #A.
         Later, in 7.42pm, the kitchens: #I is talking with #A, #B, #G, #H.
         They are making small talk about The Ashes.
         #A segues to divulging that {MARXIST STUDENT} was in a Marxist reading group back at Balliol.
         #I can tell #A is misinformed about #K being the 'MARXIST STUDENT' in their midst (this is actually #I themself!).
         The conversation takes place behind closed doors, with no one else around. No one overhears.
         * MARXIST STUDENT: #K.

         #I, confronting #F directly, segues to insinuating {SOVIET GRANDEE} is a party higher-up with distinctly Soviet leanings.
         #I has a longstanding vendetta against #F.
         The conversation takes place one-on-one. No one overhears.
         * SOVIET GRANDEE: #F.
         Later, in 7.10pm, the downstairs: #J is talking with someone out of sight.
         They are joking they'd happily fabricate evidence against {COLLEAGUE} if they didn't have to work with them anymore.
         #J segues to asserting that the only people testifying against the cabinet have their own eyes on the leadership (a rumour hitherto unheard by #I).
         The conversation takes place with no one else around. Still, #I overhears.
         * STAR WITNESS: UNIDENTIFIED.
         Later, in 7.11pm, the corridor: #I is talking with #F, #R, #S.
         They are making small talk about The Ashes.
         #F segues to divulging that {MARXIST STUDENT} was in a Marxist reading group back at Balliol.
         #I can tell #F is lying about #H being the 'MARXIST STUDENT' in their midst (earlier, #I told #F this was actually #K).
         The conversation takes place openly. Still, no one overhears.
         * MARXIST STUDENT: #H.
         Later, in 7.22pm, the downstairs: #H is talking with #J.
         They are asserting that the only people testifying against the cabinet have their own eyes on the leadership.
         #H segues to worrying about threats to the party, within and without.
         The conversation takes place one-on-one. Still, #I overhears.
         Later, in 7.56pm, the drawing room: #I is talking with #F, #R.
         They are joking they'd happily fabricate evidence against {COLLEAGUE} if they didn't have to work with them anymore.
         #F segues to implying that {#K}'s 'mystery witness' is none other than {STAR WITNESS} (a rumour hitherto unheard by #I).
         The conversation takes place openly. Still, no one overhears.
         * #K: #K.
         * STAR WITNESS: #J.

         #H segues to pondering why we've all been convened here tonight.
         The conversation takes place one-on-one. Still, #I overhears.

         They are spreading that several party grandees - {GRANDEE #1} and {GRANDEE #2} amongst them - are losing confidence in {#a}.
         #T segues to suggesting {#A} organised this evening as his grand return to politics.
